var camera, scene, renderer, light; var link; //Ball texture image var linkPyr1, linkPyr2, linkPyr3; //Pyramid texture images var linkGlass; //Glass window texture var linkBackGrd; //Background texture image setlink(); var sphere; var glassSphere; var plane; var pyramid; var ballSpeed = 0; var pyramidZ = -250; var varicolorMaterial; init(); function init() { camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera( 70, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 1, 1000 ); camera.position.z = 400; scene = new THREE.Scene(); var geometry1 = new THREE.SphereGeometry( 109, 32, 32 ); var ballMat1 = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial( { map: THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkGlass), transparent: true, opacity: 1} ); ballMat1.transparent = true; glassSphere = new THREE.Mesh( geometry1, ballMat1 ); scene.add( glassSphere ); //-----Sphere var geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry( 110, 32, 32 ); //var redMat = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial( { color: 0xff3300, specular: 0x555555, shininess: 30 } ); var ballMat = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial( { map: THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(link), transparent: true, opacity: 1} ); ballMat.transparent = true; sphere = new THREE.Mesh( geometry, ballMat ); scene.add( sphere ); //-----Pyramid //varicolorMaterial = new THREE.MeshNormalMaterial( { color: 0x2554C7, transparent: true, opacity: 1 } ); varicolorMaterial = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial( { map: THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkPyr1), transparent: true, opacity: 1} ); //var wireframeMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial( { color: 0x000000, wireframe: true, transparent: true } ); var multiMaterial = [ varicolorMaterial ]; pyramid = THREE.SceneUtils.createMultiMaterialObject( // radiusAtTop, radiusAtBottom, height, segmentsAroundRadius, segmentsAlongHeight, new THREE.CylinderGeometry( 0, 80, 100, 3, 1 ), //new THREE.TetrahedronGeometry(80), multiMaterial ); pyramid.position.set(5, -20, pyramidZ); scene.add( pyramid ); //-----Light light = new THREE.AmbientLight( 0xffffff ); // soft white light scene.add( light ); var dirLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 1); dirLight.position.set(100, 100, 0); scene.add(dirLight); var dirLight1 = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 1); dirLight1.position.set(100, 100, 200); //scene.add(dirLight1); //-----Background var planeGeom = new THREE.PlaneGeometry( 900, 600, 32 ); var planeMat = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial( { map: THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkBackGrd), transparent: true, opacity: 1} ); plane = new THREE.Mesh( planeGeom, planeMat ); scene.add( plane ); renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer(); //renderer.setClearColor ( 0x000000, 0.7 ); //renderer.shadowMapEnabled = true; renderer.setPixelRatio( window.devicePixelRatio ); renderer.setSize( window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight ); document.body.appendChild( renderer.domElement ); window.addEventListener( 'resize', onWindowResize, false ); renderer.render( scene, camera ); setTimeout(function (){renderer.render( scene, camera );}, 100); sphere.rotation.y = 0; pyramid.rotation.x = Math.PI; pyramid.rotation.y = 2*Math.PI; varicolorMaterial.opacity = 1; var zSleep = 0; var opacitySleep = 2000; var xSleep = 2000; var ySleep = 0; var waitTime = 7000; animate(); var waitCheck = true; var rnd = 0; window.onclick = function() { if (waitCheck == true){ setTimeout(function (){ rnd = Math.round(Math.random() * 2); if (rnd == 0){ varicolorMaterial.map = THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkPyr1); } if (rnd == 1){ varicolorMaterial.map = THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkPyr2); } if (rnd == 2){ varicolorMaterial.map = THREE.ImageUtils.loadTexture(linkPyr3); } }, 2000); ballSpeed = 0.02; if (sphere.rotation.y >= Math.PI){ sphere.rotation.y = -Math.PI; } if (pyramid.rotation.x >= 3*Math.PI){ //pyramid.rotation.x = -Math.PI; setTimeout(function (){ pyramid.rotation.x = Math.PI; }, xSleep); xSleep = 2000; } if (pyramid.rotation.y >= 4*Math.PI){ pyramid.rotation.y = 0; setTimeout(function (){ pyramid.rotation.y = 2*Math.PI; }, ySleep); ySleep = 2000; } if (pyramidZ >= -900){ setTimeout(function (){ pyramidZ = -900; pyramid.position.set(5, -20, pyramidZ); }, zSleep); zSleep = 2000; } if (varicolorMaterial.opacity >= 1){ varicolorMaterial.opacity = 0.9; setTimeout(function (){ varicolorMaterial.opacity = 0; }, opacitySleep); opacitySleep = 4700; } waitCheck = false; setTimeout(function (){ waitCheck = true}, waitTime); waitTime = 8200; } } } function onWindowResize() { camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight; camera.updateProjectionMatrix(); renderer.setSize( window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight ); } function animate() { requestAnimationFrame( animate ); //sphere.rotation.x += 0.005; if (sphere.rotation.y < Math.PI){ sphere.rotation.y += ballSpeed; } if (pyramid.rotation.x < 3*Math.PI){ pyramid.rotation.x += ballSpeed; } if (pyramid.rotation.y < 4*Math.PI){ pyramid.rotation.y += ballSpeed; } if (pyramidZ < -250){ pyramidZ += 2; pyramid.position.set(5, -20, pyramidZ); } if (varicolorMaterial.opacity < 1){ varicolorMaterial.opacity += 0.005; } renderer.render( scene, camera ); } //Ball texture image function setlink(){ link =
